| [Decisioning Logic / Process - Customers Segmented Weighting - Tagging weight](https://feedback.frill.co/b/4q0qxv2r/frillco-customer-ideas/decisioning-logic-process-cust)<br>决策逻辑/流程——客户分段赋权——标签权重 | This idea would allow the product to develop far beyond a method of feedback and announcements and move it into a process based product which saves large amount of times.<br>Generally Support Vs Marketing Vs Development is a huge task to manage. Marketing want new features, support want bugs fixed and Development want to know what they should do! Having customers segments and weighting on their votes would allow us to develop a system in which this tool helps us with our decision making.<br>For example: Bug 1 (Tech Lead says needs fix 10 points, Support say 15 customers have the issue 30 points)<br>Feature 1 (29 customers have the same need)<br>Feature 2 (35 customers have the same need)<br>Within a decision making context the 35 customers needs may be seen by the CEO and development pushed (feature 2), but in relality Bug 1 is a far more urgent matter.<br>This combined with tags for bugs and requests (Dealbreaker, I'd love to have this, Stops my workflow) etc. would make some very complicated decisions very easy!<br><br>这个想法将使产品的发展远远超出反馈和公告的方法，并将其转变为基于流程的产品，从而节省大量时间。<br>一般来说，支持、营销、开发是一项艰巨的管理任务。营销人员想要新功能，支持人员想要修复错误，开发人员想要知道他们应该做什么！对客户进行细分并权衡他们的投票将使我们能够开发一个系统，在该系统中该工具可以帮助我们做出决策。<br>例如：Bug 1（技术主管说需要修复 10 分，支持人员说 15 个客户有问题 30 分）<br>特点1（29个客户有相同需求）<br>特征2（35个客户有相同需求）<br>在决策环境中，CEO 可能会看到 35 个客户的需求并推动开发（功能 2），但实际上 Bug 1 是一个更为紧迫的问题。<br>这与错误和请求的标签相结合（Dealbreaker，我很想拥有这个，停止我的工作流程）等将使一些非常复杂的决定变得非常容易！ | 4 | 0 |

| [Confirmation on-screen and in email when an idea is submitted in the widget](https://feedback.frill.co/b/4q0qxv2r/frillco-customer-ideas/confirmation-on-screen-and-in-email-when-an-idea-is-submitted-in-the-widget)<br>在小部件中提交想法时，会在屏幕上和电子邮件中进行确认 | When a new idea is submitted in the widget, it goes to the next section based on the settings for that widget. This is an ideal time to thank the user for the effort and time to submit the request/idea, and to set expectations about what happens next.  We prefer not to send any emails about approval, and the only public-facing part of Frill is the widget to submit an idea - so without any confirmation screen and/or email, the user has no way to know their idea went through or what to expect next.<br>We would like these settings to be handled per widget as we use these for multiple use cases that would need totally different confirmation screens and emails.<br><br>当在小部件中提交新想法时，它将根据该小部件的设置进入下一部分。没有提交的确认屏幕，也没有关于提交的后续电子邮件。<br>我们两者都想要。  这是感谢用户为提交请求/想法而付出的努力和时间，并对接下来发生的事情设定期望的理想时机。  我们不想发送任何有关批准的电子邮件，Frill 唯一面向公众的部分是提交想法的小部件 - 因此，如果没有任何确认屏幕和/或电子邮件，用户无法知道他们的想法已经通过或接下来会发生什么。<br>我们希望每个小部件处理这些设置，因为我们将这些设置用于需要完全不同的确认屏幕和电子邮件的多个用例。 | 3 | 0 |
